  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_85ccaff9-c6e7-4aca-9dd7-c37e5e38911c'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText7562031362442671313" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Don’t date your bodyguard.</i>
</b><br /><b>It was the one rule he had to break.</b><br /><br />Maximoff Hale is a force of nature. A ship unwilling to be steered. Headstrong, resilient, and wholly responsible — the twenty-two-year-old alpha billionaire can handle his unconventional life. By noon, lunch can turn into a mob of screaming fans. By two, his face is all over the internet. <br /><br />Born into one of the most famous families in the country, his celebrity status began at birth. <br /><br />He is certified American royalty. <br /><br />When he’s assigned a new 24/7 bodyguard, he comes face-to-face with the worst case scenario: being attached to the tattooed, MMA-trained, Yale graduate who’s known for “going rogue” in the security team — and who fills 1/3 of Maximoff's sexual fantasies. <br /><br />Twenty-seven-year-old Farrow Keene has one job: protect Maximoff Hale. Flirting, dating, and hot sex falls far, far out of the boundary of his bodyguard duties and into “termination” territory. But when feelings surface, protecting the sexy-as-sin, stubborn celebrity becomes increasingly complicated. <br /><br />Together, boundaries blur, and being exposed could mean catastrophic consequences for both.<br /><br /><b>The Like Us series is a true series, one continuous timeline, that follows a family of wealthy celebrities and the people that protect them. <i>Damaged Like Us</i> can be read and enjoyed without reading any of Krista &amp; Becca's other novels.</b></span>

You don't need to read any of our previous novels in order to read Damaged Like Us -- it stands on its own as the start to a brand new series about American royalty & the bodyguards sworn to protect them.<br/><br/><b>*** 2017 UPDATE ***</b><br/><br/>The blurb and the release date are here! P.S. the Like Us serie</span>
  <span id="freeText18186798772551167514" style="display:none"> <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Damaged-Like-Us-Book-ebook/dp/B071KYP7YT/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1498540643&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=damaged+like+us" rel="nofollow noopener"> IT'S LIVE!</a> Happy Reading, everyone!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498576666i/23139294.png" width="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Krista &amp; I hope you enjoy all the OMFG moments, happy feelings, laugh-out-loud parts, and the heartfelt bonds! P.S. the Like Us series is post-college! So you won't be reading about the characters in a college setting. They're adulting and navigating romance amid being American royalty! :D We're soooo excited to start this adventure with all of you, and we hope you join us on the wild ride that is the Like Us series!! <br><br>You can read the Like Us series without having read any of our other novels beforehand! <br><br>OLD UPDATE: <br><br>Some details about the Like Us series are in the back of <i> Addicted After All </i> (Addicted #3) *wink wink* You don't need to read the Addicted series or Calloway Sisters spin-off series to read <i> Damaged Like Us</i>, though little parts of the world may make you giddy if you've read them beforehand. <br><br>Very briefly: this is about a group of twenty-somethings raised in the public eye, with no control over their labels or how people perceive them. With a strong focus on family, romance, love, and college -- you'll witness three people tied by blood navigate life. Only difference between them and you: they're doing it all underneath the brightest, hottest -- sometimes unbearable -- spotlight. <br><br><b> ** RELEASE DATE UPDATE ** </b><br><br>Coming Spring 2017! If you're wondering why the delay, it's because we decided to add Fuel the Fire, Long Way Down, and Some Kind of Perfect before releasing the Like Us series. All three of those books are now available, and the Like Us series, starting with Damaged Like Us, will begin in 2017 :)</span>

<div id="review_1111819804" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1111819804" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1111819804?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2017-five-stars">2017-five-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1111819804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13913790884433230661"><b>5 stars!!!</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/19601116_10103944646458748_6266696057322551869_n_zpsgfuiz9qo.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499421959i/23229902._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 19601116_10103944646458748_6266696057322551869_n_zpsgfuiz9qo.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Reading another book with my favorite fictional family in it feels like coming home. Loren and Lily Hale are probably my #1 favorite book couple ever. <i>Damaged Like Us</i> is their son, Maximoff Hale’s, book. This can be read as a stand-alone, but I think for those of us that are huge Addicted fans, it will be even more special! <br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>You all know me as Maximoff Hale. CEO of a nonprofit charity, one-time philosophy major, competitive swimmer, son of a sex addict mother and recovering</blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText13913790884433230661" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!!!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/19601116_10103944646458748_6266696057322551869_n_zpsgfuiz9qo.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499421959i/23229902._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 19601116_10103944646458748_6266696057322551869_n_zpsgfuiz9qo.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Reading another book with my favorite fictional family in it feels like coming home. Loren and Lily Hale are probably my #1 favorite book couple ever. <i>Damaged Like Us</i> is their son, Maximoff Hale’s, book. This can be read as a stand-alone, but I think for those of us that are huge Addicted fans, it will be even more special! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>You all know me as Maximoff Hale. CEO of a nonprofit charity, one-time philosophy major, competitive swimmer, son of a sex addict mother and recovering alcoholic father, and the steadfast older brother to three and cousin to eleven</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br>Moffy was born into fame. Privacy is something he’s used to not having. A body guard is something he’s had his entire life, so it’s nothing new to him. When Moffy’s bodyguard he’s had for the longest time retires, he’s a bit anxious to get a new one. You spend a lot of time with this person and he was used to who he had. He was comfortable. Farrow Keene, his teenage crush who used to be his mother’s bodyguard, is not someone he wants protecting him. But that’s who he ends up with. <br><br>The chemistry between these two was hot from the start. You could feel the sexual tension between Farrow and Moffy from the beginning. I loved their banter and connection. I loved that Farrow really saw Moffy, who he was, not just as a famous person. Being with Farrow changed Moffy. The sparks between them flew. I didn’t know how the twins would do writing a m/m romance, but I thought they did a fantastic job. <br><br>  Moffy is the oldest of the Hale kids and since he’s the oldest, he’s always been the one his siblings and cousins turn to. I love the family dynamic in this book. Getting to see the old Addicted gang, and the new generation made my heart so happy. I loved the relationship between Moffy and his cousin, Jane. I can’t wait to get her book as well! I was a little anxious about Farrow at first, but I was so glad I ended up loving him as much as Moffy. <br><br>The writing was spectacular as always. I loved the little quips and pop culture references. There are always lines in a Ritchie book that make me laugh or put a huge smile on my face. My favorite one in the book was from Lily- <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Moffy!” Her mouth drops. “You’re a Hufflepuff. Be nice.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i>  <i>Damaged Like Us</i> is a book I would recommend to all fans of the Addicted series, m/m lovers, and lovers of romance alike. It was a great start to this next generation series and I can’t wait to read more!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/19601353_10103944646473718_7101181671632165338_n_zpst9tv7z0q.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499421959i/23229903._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 19601353_10103944646473718_7101181671632165338_n_zpst9tv7z0q.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13913790884433230661" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2043599971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11411262577752921685">DNF @ 50%<br/><br/>If I'm bored and frustrated halfway through, it's time to call it quits.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500215984ra/23310676.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I loathed the narrative style. I don't want to be talked at. It's like the date who won't stop talking about themselves, and you're like, Check, please. <br/><br/><b>Don't TELL me; SHOW ME. Breaking the fourth wall is almost always a no-no in romantic fiction.</b><br/><br/>If I need a freaking Excel spreadsheet to keep track of the secondary characters, there are too many. I tried to read this book as a standalone, and it was an epic fail. <br/><br/>I </span>
  <span id="freeText11411262577752921685" style="display:none">DNF @ 50%<br><br>If I'm bored and frustrated halfway through, it's time to call it quits.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500215984ra/23310676.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loathed the narrative style. I don't want to be talked at. It's like the date who won't stop talking about themselves, and you're like, Check, please. <br><br><b>Don't TELL me; SHOW ME. Breaking the fourth wall is almost always a no-no in romantic fiction.</b><br><br>If I need a freaking Excel spreadsheet to keep track of the secondary characters, there are too many. I tried to read this book as a standalone, and it was an epic fail. <br><br>I disliked Maximoff pretty much on sight. He's arrogant, flippant, and famous for being famous. <b>The whole rich celebrity lifestyle was way OTT. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500215984ra/23310677.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm no expert on the rich and fabulous, but Prince Harry somehow manages to live a fairly low-key life, yet no one in Maximoff's extended family can even sneeze without like twenty paparazzi documenting the moment. <br><br>Plus, both MCs are one-dimensional and have ridunkulous names. I can't get behind a guy named Moffy. I just can't.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11411262577752921685" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2313000001" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14664920683413631540"><b>4.25 Stars</b><br/><br/>I will literally - literally - read anything the Ritchie sisters write, <i>especially</i> anything about the Calloway/Cobalt/Meadows clan. <br/><br/>For serious though, I LOVE these families and I LOVE these characters. <br/><br/>This one was no different - and an MM on top of that! Woot woot. <br/><br/>I really enjoyed Maximoff and Farrow and I can't wait for the next. <br/>Hell, it even made me feel like going back and re-reading the whole series. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520120161i/25157460._SX540_.jpg' width='496' height='279' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>*My Maximoff</i><br/><br/><a href='https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118337i/22283577.png' width='40' height='40' alt='Follow us on facebook' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118337i/22283578.png' width='40' height='40' alt='Follow us on instagram' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='http://steamyreads.net/youtube/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490120705i/22283756.png' width='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='http://www.steamyreads.net' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118159i/22283551._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a></span>
  <span id="freeText14664920683413631540" style="display:none"><b>4.25 Stars</b><br><br>I will literally - literally - read anything the Ritchie sisters write, <i>especially</i> anything about the Calloway/Cobalt/Meadows clan. <br><br>For serious though, I LOVE these families and I LOVE these characters. <br><br>This one was no different - and an MM on top of that! Woot woot. <br><br>I really enjoyed Maximoff and Farrow and I can't wait for the next. <br>Hell, it even made me feel like going back and re-reading the whole series. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520120161i/25157460._SX540_.jpg" width="496" height="279" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>*My Maximoff</i><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1333611617?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=let-me-have-your-babies">let-me-have-your-babies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying">i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1333611617" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1820903623063376272"><b>CURRENTLY FREEEEEEEEEEE!!!!!! <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://amzn.to/2SeEQh4'>https://amzn.to/2SeEQh4</a> </b><br/><br/><br/>*brain error recognition*<br/>*too happy to even properly form words*<br/>*too emotional I feel like flying above the sky*<br/><br/>HOW AM I EVEN GOING TO REVIEW THIS?!?!? *INHALES, EXHALES* okay, okay. Let me try to express my love for this. (WARNING: FAN-GIRLING AND GUSHING IS COMING YOUR WAY)<br/><br/>Not to be dramatic, but like, this is the best book ever. Really. This may be my FAVORITE by Krista and Becca Ritchie. I don't think I've ever felt so alive after finishi</span>
  <span id="freeText1820903623063376272" style="display:none"><b>CURRENTLY FREEEEEEEEEEE!!!!!! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://amzn.to/2SeEQh4">https://amzn.to/2SeEQh4</a> </b><br><br><br>*brain error recognition*<br>*too happy to even properly form words*<br>*too emotional I feel like flying above the sky*<br><br>HOW AM I EVEN GOING TO REVIEW THIS?!?!? *INHALES, EXHALES* okay, okay. Let me try to express my love for this. (WARNING: FAN-GIRLING AND GUSHING IS COMING YOUR WAY)<br><br>Not to be dramatic, but like, this is the best book ever. Really. This may be my FAVORITE by Krista and Becca Ritchie. I don't think I've ever felt so alive after finishing a book. <br><br>This was UN-PUT-DOWN-ABLE. I'm talking bring the kindle with you to pee, to eat, to cook type of ‘can't put it down.’<br><br>I’m going to try give a short summary on these characters so anyone who hasn’t read the Addicted Series series has some background information - but without spoiling too much on this book or the Addicted Series. <br><br><b>Maximoff Hale</b>, in his words: 22 year old CEO of a nonprofit charity, one-time philosophy major, competitive swimmer, son of a sex addict mother and recovering alcoholic father, and the steadfast older brother to three and cousin to eleven. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498674797i/23150887._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/4SPbsoM" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498674268ra/23150816.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>He’s wealthy. He’s head strong. He adores his family. He’s known all around the world because of his parents and relatives. He’s so famous, in fact, he’s had a 24/7 bodyguard his whole life. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Our fame burns. And burns. None of us need to stoke the flames for it to stay lit. And me—fame is my friend and foe. It’s a part of me. A tangible thing that lives inside of me. This is the only life I’ve ever lived. It’s the only life I know.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Enter <b>Farrow Keene</b>: 27 year old, tattooed, Yale graduate known as the “rule breaker” in Maximoff’s family’s security force and his new bodyguard.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498674905i/23150891._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/YPBf5AL" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498674268ra/23150817.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Fun fact: Maximoff has had a crush on Farrow since his teen years. So when he learns that Farrow is going to be with him from sun up to sun down, he isn’t too thrilled. They BOTH know doing anything with a bodyguard or client is off limits, but they aren’t so sure they can ignore and resist the feelings they have.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>His know-it-all smile fucking kills me, and I swear he’s one second from saying, <i>do you like that?</i> And I think, <i>too damn much.</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br>_<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>My gaze latches intensely onto his. And his brown eyes plaster onto my green. So strongly that I’m drop-dead positive we’re forcing ourselves not to look lower. Not to our lips, not to our bodies. Not to any forbidden place that’d cause disaster. I try to master restraint, but my eyes say what my mouth can’t. <i>Kiss me.</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Take the already mounting sexual tension from their past, plus the fact that these two spend almost ALL of their time together, and what you get is one HOT AS HELL forbidden love story. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I’m watched and observed all the time. By strangers. By cameramen. By people. And never, <i>never</i> have I come undone. Until now, until his eyes feel like hands, and I want them all over me. </blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Le8RWiC" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498674973ra/23150894.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And the banter between these two was so freaking entertaining:<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “Wow,” Farrow breathes, “I rocked your teenage world, didn’t I?”<br> I flash him an annoyed smile. “I’m limp now. Thank you for that.”<br>Farrow glances at the hard outline in my jeans. “Your erection says you’re a fucking liar.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Guess who's going to re-read this over and OVER until the next book is out. <br>Clue: It's me. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I’m hooked by the way he’s staring deeply at me. Like I’m a fantasy. Like I’m something made of heaven and stars that he’s dreamt of—and I never thought to ask what a celebrity who could have anyone in the fucking world fantasizes about. And I wonder how long it’s been me. </blockquote>
</b><br><br>But to be serious for a moment here, these authors are a force to be reckoned with. 13 books later, and I have LOVED and given every single one of them 5 stars. Do you understand what that means for a picky reader like me?? No one creates characters as unique as they do, no one writes stories as original as their stories, and NEVER do I feel so immediately connected to a book than when I start one of theirs. In a book world that has cliché after cliché, re-used story-line after re-used story-line, they ALWAYS STAND OUT in the best way. <br><br><b>This was EVERYTHING. Funny, INSANELY romantic, SCORCHING HOT, intense, and completely addictive.</b> These girls know how to write a book that hooks you from page one and does not let go until the very end. And even once you're done, you'll want to re-read this again and again just to capture those feelings one more time.<br><br>And kudos to Krista &amp; Becca for making this story completely unpredictable and something that totally exceeded all of my expectations. <br><br>*side note (<i>wow I really can’t shut up about this book, can I? If you’re still reading this review – I adore you</i>) - the side characters in this are out of this world entertaining. Fans of the Addicted Series will LOVE getting to see all of the beloved characters again, and everyone will without a doubt fall head over heels for the group of bodyguards. (I’m already calling dibs on Thatcher. Italian and an alpha bodyguard? MINE!) <br><br>Damaged Like Us is OUT NOW!!!!!! |<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2tv3bHj">http://amzn.to/2tv3bHj</a><br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="Corina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8905971-corina"><img alt="Corina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580618612p2/8905971.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1107772196?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Corina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Corina" href="/user/show/8905971-corina">Corina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8905971-corina?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8905971-corina?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1107772196" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14853088141763260165">Damaged Like Us is the beginning of an epic series. I never thought that anyone could replace Rose and Connor, from Kiss the Sky, in my affections, but Maximoff and Farrow did so with such ease, I was shocked how fast I fell for both of them.<br/><br/>If you haven’t read this series, it’s one of the most unique contemporary romance series there is. Different in every sense. Now, since the author’s are giving the second generation a chance to shine, the expectations are unbelievably high.<br/><br/>For me, Maximoff a</span>
  <span id="freeText14853088141763260165" style="display:none">Damaged Like Us is the beginning of an epic series. I never thought that anyone could replace Rose and Connor, from Kiss the Sky, in my affections, but Maximoff and Farrow did so with such ease, I was shocked how fast I fell for both of them.<br /><br />If you haven’t read this series, it’s one of the most unique contemporary romance series there is. Different in every sense. Now, since the author’s are giving the second generation a chance to shine, the expectations are unbelievably high.<br /><br />For me, Maximoff and Farrow, the author’s first go at a MM romance, are the ultimate goal of a great, charismatic and addicting couple. I have read this book a couple times already, and it has not yet lost any of it’s charm.<br /><br />I’m in love with these two – utterly in love.<br /><br />Maximoff and Farrow have by far one of the most fulfilling and perfect relationship I have witnessed so far. The push and pull is utterly unique, none gives an inch, always challenges the other, and it all is like catnip for me. I can’t get enough of it.<br /><br />Before you start with this series, I would suggest read their parent’s story first. There are just too many characters in this series, to jump into it without the backstory. And you want to read the crazy backstories, because as I said above, it’s incredibly fascinating and different.<br /><br />___________________________________<br /><a href="https://thebrowneyedbookworm.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more reviews and book recommendations on my blog.</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebrowneyedbookworm/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find me on Bookstagram.</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14853088141763260165" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1003663723" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1003663723" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1003663723?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=mm">mm</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1003663723" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7145601770238199989"><b>4 STARS</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>I broke the unbreakable rule. Don’t fuck your client. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499048080ra/23185070.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>So....confession time...<br/>*whispers*<br/>This is the first book I've read by these authors.<br/>*ducks head in shame*<br/>Yes, yes, I'm wearing the cone of shame as I write this, mkay? So quit looking at me with those judgy eyes already. I realize what I've been missing out on and currently kicking my own ass. Cut me some slack here. <br/><br/>I have all of their books on my TBR but for some unknown to me reason just never got around to reading them.</span>
  <span id="freeText7145601770238199989" style="display:none"><b>4 STARS</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I broke the unbreakable rule. Don’t fuck your client. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499048080ra/23185070.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So....confession time...<br>*whispers*<br>This is the first book I've read by these authors.<br>*ducks head in shame*<br>Yes, yes, I'm wearing the cone of shame as I write this, mkay? So quit looking at me with those judgy eyes already. I realize what I've been missing out on and currently kicking my own ass. Cut me some slack here. <br><br>I have all of their books on my TBR but for some unknown to me reason just never got around to reading them. I can tell you that I will be rectifying that HUGE mistake immediately but devouring their entire backlist. But enough about that. Let's talk about this book.<br><br>Firstly, let's address something right off the bat. I could clearly see that I was missing quite a bit of backstory with the secondary characters here as this is a spin off from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/124271-calloway-sisters" rel="nofollow noopener">Calloway Sisters series</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/103875-addicted" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted series</a>. As a matter of fact, Maximoff is the son of Lily and Lo. This series introduces all of the children and I was absolutely smitten with it. It took me a bit to wrap my mind around all of the connections, but the authors did a fantastic job really introducing all the secondary characters so that I never felt lost.<br><br>Born into one of the most famous families in the country, Maximoff Hale is pretty much American royalty. His father is just as known for his past alcoholism as his business, and his mother is just as famous for being a sex addict as her family's business, he's used to living his life under a microscope. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">fame is my friend and foe. It’s a part of me. A tangible thing that lives inside of me. This is the only life I’ve ever lived . It’s the only life I know.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Privacy is a luxury that he'll never have and a real relationship is something that he'll never experience because he'll never expose someone to what he goes through on a daily basis. A life of NDAs and meaningless one night stands is what he's used to. <br><br>When he learns that he'll be getting a new bodyguard, he's not exactly thrilled. The Hale bodyguards are more then employees, they're a 24/7 presence and friends and confidents. When he finds out that his new bodyguard is the star of all his teenage fantasies, a crush he never got over, and a man that he's still uncontrollably attracted to, life becomes a little more complicated.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">He’s made permanent camp in my cerebral cortex and cock, and I don’t know how to extract him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499048149ra/23185086.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The more time they spend together, the more difficult it becomes to deny the overbearing sexual tension that brews between them. Admittedly, that delicious tension was one of my favorite parts about the book. Every time these two so much as had a conversation, you could feel the chemistry crackle and burn. And their first kiss? Holy mother of god! It was hotter than any sex scene. Swear.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Farrow returns the aroused, taut sentiment. Our short breaths are the only true noise. <br>The headiest exchange of my life. <br>Undeniable. <br>He leans forward, his lips an inch from mine. And very deeply, very huskily, he whispers, “What do you want, Maximoff ?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>There's a lot that happens here that goes beyond the main couple. While the romance is absolutely the center focus, you get introduced to a slew of secondary characters. While usually this may cause me to struggle, I felt like it just connected me to these characters even more. I loved the bond that these siblings and cousins share.<br><br>But Maximoff and Farrow most definitely stole the show. I loved these two together. I loved Maximoff's intensity and Farrow's easy going flintiness. He's such a fan chapter. His presence totally sucks you in. The authors created such a vivid character with him. All of his aneurism, eye brow quirks and gum popping served to endear me to him more and more. And when these two guys get together? Yowza!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">We’re like lightning and thunder, inherently different but alike enough to share the same sky.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>It was the perfect blend of swoon and steam. I adored these two together and I already can't wait for more. The parents have quite a bit of redeeming to do after what happens at the end of this book. I love that we get a satisfying HFN to tide us over until the next book. Now if you'll excuse me, I'm off to binge the Ritchie's entire backlist.<br><br><i>Huge GIANT thank you to the authors for gifting me this book &lt;3</i><br><br><b>Find me on:<br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/DirtyGirlRomance?" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525717.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow me on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/DirtyGrlRomance" target="twitter" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525718.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow Me on Twitter" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="http://www.dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525719.png" width="40" height="40" alt="blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7145601770238199989" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1986958179" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17406476413241543821">Re-read 9/24/19<br/><br/>I am a huge fan of these authors.... Like screaming fangirling huge !!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498642547ra/23146273.gif' alt='tumblr_mku0emDJcB1qf8btso1_250.gif (246×230)' width='172' height='161' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So imagine how I felt when I found out that my favorite authors didn't only write a spin-off of one of my favorite series....but they also made it an MM one !!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470781674ra/19964533.gif' alt=' happy dream joy cinderella disney quote GIF' width='290' height='217' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>That's right !! This is Moffy's (Maximoff) story and we get us some man on man action <3<br/><br/>Now first things first... The authors say that this story can be read as a stand-alone and I agree...sort off. If you haven't read the "Addicted" and "Calloway" series</span>
  <span id="freeText17406476413241543821" style="display:none">Re-read 9/24/19<br><br>I am a huge fan of these authors.... Like screaming fangirling huge !!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498642547ra/23146273.gif" alt="tumblr_mku0emDJcB1qf8btso1_250.gif (246×230)" width="172" height="161" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So imagine how I felt when I found out that my favorite authors didn't only write a spin-off of one of my favorite series....but they also made it an MM one !!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470781674ra/19964533.gif" alt=" happy dream joy cinderella disney quote GIF" width="290" height="217" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's right !! This is Moffy's (Maximoff) story and we get us some man on man action &lt;3<br><br>Now first things first... The authors say that this story can be read as a stand-alone and I agree...sort off. If you haven't read the "Addicted" and "Calloway" series, you can still read this book and follow the storyline. I do think though, that this book is so much more enjoyable if you have read the previous series. These families went through a lot to get where they are now. I don't think you can fully grasp how and why Moffy came to be who he is today if you skip the other series. So my personal advice would be to read the other books....they are so freaking good !!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498642547ra/23146274.gif" alt="141008010250836618.gif (500×240)" width="390" height="187" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, this book ends in a HFN. It is a new series and there will be another book(s) about this couple... No cliffy, so don't worry ;)<br><br>Now about the story...and I will try to keep the spoilers low...<br><br>Moffy is the son of Lily Calloway and Loren Hale. His parents are extremely famous...and not always in a good way. His mom is the daughter of the founder of "Fizz", a soda that surpassed coca-cola. She is also a sexaddict...which is how she became famous because her personal life was leaked to the press. His father, Loren Hale, is also very well known because of his last name, since its the name of a famous baby line. He is a recovering alcoholic. They didn't have it easy and they had a lot of hate thrown their way...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498642547ra/23146275.gif" alt="tenor.gif (498×280)" width="336" height="189" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story isn't about Moffy's parents though, since they already have their own books. They do make a small appearance.<br><br>This story is about Moffy and the fact that he himself has been very very famous, since the moment he was born. Everything about him is public knowledge. He can't go anywhere without being hounded by fans, haters and the press. All of this is the reason that Moffy needs a bodyguard 24/7. Since his old bodyguard is retiring, he is getting a new one....and he isn't exactly happy about this fact.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466447217ra/19480737.gif" alt="no new girl frustrated oh no schmidt GIF" width="399" height="225" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Farrow has been fodder for Maximoff's spank bank since Moffy was 16 years old. He is the son of their family doctor and after finishing his medical degree, he decided that security was much more his thing. He has been Lily's bodyguard for the last 3 years and now he is being assigned as Moffy's personal protection.<br><br>Moffy is bisexual and he has been out for a long time. The only thing he isn't open about towards the public and the press are his hookups. He has no idea how he is gonna function with his "wet dream" protecting him and watching him 24 hours a day......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498642547ra/23146276.gif" alt="10649278.gif (483×171)" width="342" height="121" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But when it becomes clear that Farrow feels the exact same way about him...all bets are off.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492084592i/22480422.jpg" alt="QNvsOQb.jpg (182×276)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think these authors did a very good job with their first MM. It was very sexy and sweet ;)<br><br>I loved catching up with all these kids that I missed so much. I loved seeing how close Moffy and Jane still were. I can't wait to read more. Like I said earlier, this book ends on a HFN, because there will be more to follow. I can only hope that all the kids get their own book (s).<br><br>Now I am gonna have to re-read the "Addicted" and the "Calloway" series again :P<br><br></span>

<div id="review_1986610089" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1986610089" />
    <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet"><img alt="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387046887p2/13567836.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1986610089?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet">Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/35047889-damaged-like-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=ex-military-security-investigator">ex-military-security-investigator</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1986610089" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2864015744231498138"><b>
  <u>Third re-read: 07.11.2020</u>
</b><br/>I found myself missing Moffy and Farrow. Hell it's been two years since my last re-read so no wonder. There's just something beautiful and pure between those two males. I adore them. The story itself, however, is a bit boring. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[I don't remember, but I hope Moffy - and Jane - doesn't forgive their family so easily for thinking they were in an incest relationship. <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>New Rating</b> - 3 *can't seem to make up my mind* stars.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 04.09</u></b></span>
  <span id="freeText2864015744231498138" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Third re-read: 07.11.2020</u>
</b><br>I found myself missing Moffy and Farrow. Hell it's been two years since my last re-read so no wonder. There's just something beautiful and pure between those two males. I adore them. The story itself, however, is a bit boring. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I don't remember, but I hope Moffy - and Jane - doesn't forgive their family so easily for thinking they were in an incest relationship. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>New Rating</b> - 3 *can't seem to make up my mind* stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 04.09.2018</u>
</b><br>I just couldn't help myself. I needed to remind myself my I liked the authors in the first place as the Addicted series didn't work <i>at all</i> for me. Plus, I've missed Maximoff and Farrow. I seriously hope we get more than 3 books for these two... because I need that. Really.<br><b>New Rating</b> - 3.5 stars ---&gt; I keep going back and forth.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1549554694ra/27029584.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I read into his words. “You think Moffy’s hot?”<br>“Everyone thinks Moffy’s hot.” Oscar rotates to me. “It’d be near impossible to find someone who says less than that. You see him. On a scale of one to ten, he’s—”<br>“Out of your league,” I say matter-of-factly. Trying not to appear territorial. My muscles contract, almost flexed, but Oscar can’t tell.<br>“More like, he’s way, way off-limits.”<br>Maybe.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 07.11.2017</u>
</b><br>I did enjoyed this re-read, however, I remember why I only gave it 3 stars; <b>it's boring</b>. Meaning, there's little (action) happening. I do still like my boys Maximoff and Farrow, and I'm excited to start book two. <b>I just hope I won't get disappointed</b>, like I did with this one. When things get boring, I start skimming, which I did in this re-read. Not good...<br><b>New Rating</b> - 3 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Some wolf scout loving*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br>I actually liked this one. I'm kinda angry with myself that I started the book before the rest of the story of Billionaire <b>Maximoff ‘Moffy’ ‘wolf scout’ Hale</b> (22) and bodyguard <b>Farrow Redford Keene</b> (27) were finished. I hate waiting you see. Maximoff is a real compassionate, loving and humble guy. He's incredible nice and only wants the best for his family. He puts his families needs over his own, and to be honest, wolf scout deserves way fucking more. Farrow is more of a laidback dude, who's blunt and says it was it is. Both are very likable characters who fit each other just perfectly. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If I’m not the hero, what am I?” Maximoff is waiting for me to call him a villain. In his comic books, that’s the dichotomy. Heroes versus villains.<br>He’s very far from one.<br>I press my lips to his jaw, his neck, and against his ear, I whisper, “You’re a prince who wants to be a knight.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I liked both of the characters and <b>I specially liked them together</b>. I'm curious to see their relationship get even <i>deeper</i>, but of course, I have to fucking wait for that. I don't want to wait. I want to see Maximoff and Farrow's journey straight away. Like read all the books after one another and finish their story so I know they got the happy ending they deserve. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“And you see being with your bodyguard as wrong. And wrong leads to bad; and bad equals unhappy in your philosophically-bound head. You realize that not everyone thinks that way, Maximoff?”<br>My brows knot. “In what universe does wrong lead to rays of fucking sunshine and happily-ever-afters, Farrow? Please, enlighten me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Overall, the story was interesting</b>, I liked the closeness of the families and I love that the bodyguards aren't just bodyguards, but more like friends (Though there was this one scene where I wanted to kill some of the family members; how dare them question Maximoff that way?). However, not much happened, so if the book had been longer, I would probably had gotten bored, but luckily it was just the perfect length.<br><br><b><u>Character List</u>:</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i>Not all characters in this list will make an appearance in the book, but most will be mentioned.<br>Ages represent the age of the character at the beginning of the book. Some characters will be older when they’re introduced, depending on their birthday.</i><br><b>THE HALES</b><br><i>Lily Calloway &amp; Loren Hale</i><br>Maximoff - 22<br>Luna – 17<br>Xander – 14<br>Kinney – 12<br><b>THE COBALTS</b><br><i>Richard Connor Cobalt &amp; Rose Calloway</i><br>Jane - 22<br>Charlie – 19<br>Beckett – 19<br>Eliot – 18<br>Tom – 17<br>Ben – 15<br>Audrey – 12<br><b>THE MEADOWS</b><br><i>Ryke Meadows &amp; Daisy Calloway</i><br>Sullivan - 19<br>Winona – 13<br><b>THE SECURITY TEAM</b><br><i>These are the bodyguards that protect the Hales, Cobalts, and Meadows.</i><br><b>Security Force Omega</b><br>Akara Kitsuwon - 25<br>Farrow Keene – 27<br>Quinn Oliveira– 20<br>Oscar Oliveira - 30<br>Paul Donnelly – 26<br><b>Security Force Epsilon</b><br>Thatcher Moretti - 27<br>Banks Moretti – 27<br>Heidi Smith – 50s<br>…and more<br><b>Security Force Alpha</b><br>Price Kepler – 40s<br>…and more. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Thoreau said, ‘Do not be too moral. You may cheat yourself out of much life. So aim above morality. Be not simply good; be good for something.’”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (NA) Contemporary Romance (M/M)<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes, so far. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Maximoff Hale &amp; Farrow Redford Keene.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Who knows.<br><b>Rating</b> - 3.5 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2042263884" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2042263884" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2042263884?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/35047889-damaged-like-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2042263884" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5994588012741993615"><b> 4 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Dear World, stop fucking with me. Sincerely, an agitated human.” </i> </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498719146i/23155080._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Maximoff Hale is the son of reality television star royalty. His entire life, he has known nothing but the spotlight, the constant nagging of the paparazzi, and has always had a body guard. But when his guard retires, Moffy is faced with having to spend his days with a new guard. He’s even more shocked when that new bodyguard ends up being his childhood crush, Farrow Keene. <br/><br/>Farrow is five years older than Moffy, and w</span>
  <span id="freeText5994588012741993615" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Dear World, stop fucking with me. Sincerely, an agitated human.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498719146i/23155080._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maximoff Hale is the son of reality television star royalty. His entire life, he has known nothing but the spotlight, the constant nagging of the paparazzi, and has always had a body guard. But when his guard retires, Moffy is faced with having to spend his days with a new guard. He’s even more shocked when that new bodyguard ends up being his childhood crush, Farrow Keene. <br><br>Farrow is five years older than Moffy, and with his father being the Hale family physician, he’s comfortable with the family. The more time he spends with his charge, the more he realizes he’s attracted to him, and the feeling seems to be mutual. The only problem? Bodyguard and charges cannot date, making anything between them forbidden.<br><br><b> <i> “Don’t you see, Maximoff? There’s a cement wall in front of you, and you’ve just been told to be satisfied with staring at it. And so you stand there, not able to see the other side.” </i> </b><br><br>I was so extremely excited for this book, not only is it a spin-off of the Addicted series, but we get an MM romance too? I was completely overjoyed and ecstatic, it’s like Christmas came in June! Finishing this book, I came to the realization of why I love books by the Ritchie twins so much: they always deliver a quality story with realistic, relatable characters and lots of feels. It’s obvious they take their time when writing a book and make sure the reader gets a story of great caliber. And Damaged Like Us follows in that same vein.<br><br>I loved both Moffy and Farrow equally, these two men were amazing! Moffy is the oldest of all the Calloway children, and because of that he falls into the role of protector. Moffy will support is siblings and cousins, would kill for them. His loyalty to his family is the most important thing to him. Farrow values his work, he knows that what he does makes a difference, and he will also do anything to keep the family safe. It’s rare that I say this about a character, but I also really dug Farrow’s demeanor, the twins did an amazing job describing him and developing him.<br><br>There were some issues near the end that I felt were rushed and kind of brushed aside. I wish that we had seen more of what came of those issues, but maybe we will see more of their impact in the next book? Or a novella? I was just shocked by the behavior of some of the characters from the original series and never really got an explanation or confrontation about it, which I really wish we had. <br><br>I love these authors, I after having read eleven works by them I can honestly say they write the best books in the indie romance community. I really enjoyed this book, it’s a fantastic start to a new series and I cannot wait to read what is to come.<br><br><b> <i> “Millions of people know me, but not like this. Not like that. I hang onto that fact like rope on a wall that blocks my view of everything. He’s how I see the other side. He’s made my life feel freer.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="5994588012741993615" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=actor-celebrity">actor-celebrity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=narrator-very-good">narrator-very-good</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2065596165" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6159265917102416099"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>DNF at 45%<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21427834.Damaged_Like_Us__Like_Us___1_' title='Damaged Like Us (Like Us, #1) by Krista Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Damaged Like Us</a> is my first book from the Ritchies (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7056935.Krista_Ritchie' title='Krista Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Krista Ritchie</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2754148.Becca_Ritchie' title='Becca Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Becca Ritchie</a>) and I really struggled with it. <br/><br/>First of all, it's billed as a stand-alone when it's ANYTHING but. You really need to have read the Calloway sister series to follow along, and even then you should have a chart or map or something. I was totally, 100% lost when it came to the characters, and I eventually gave up trying to figure out who was who. <br/><br/>I really enjoyed the narration from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8279965.J_F__Harding' title='J.F. Harding' rel='nofollow noopener'>J.F. Harding</a>, who is </span>
  <span id="freeText6159265917102416099" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>DNF at 45%<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21427834.Damaged_Like_Us__Like_Us___1_" title="Damaged Like Us (Like Us, #1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Damaged Like Us</a> is my first book from the Ritchies (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7056935.Krista_Ritchie" title="Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Krista Ritchie</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2754148.Becca_Ritchie" title="Becca Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Becca Ritchie</a>) and I really struggled with it. <br><br>First of all, it's billed as a stand-alone when it's ANYTHING but. You really need to have read the Calloway sister series to follow along, and even then you should have a chart or map or something. I was totally, 100% lost when it came to the characters, and I eventually gave up trying to figure out who was who. <br><br>I really enjoyed the narration from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8279965.J_F__Harding" title="J.F. Harding" rel="nofollow noopener">J.F. Harding</a>, who is a rock star in my book, but the narration from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4419118.Alexander_Cendese" title="Alexander Cendese" rel="nofollow noopener">Alexander Cendese</a> really bothered me. Alexander Cendese has a great sort of "tough" voice, but it didn't fit for the son of super upper class doctors, IMO. <br><br>I often struggle with contemporary romance, but it seems like M/M romance from primarily M/F authors tends to bother me the most. I just didn't buy anything about the story, and I had no problems with my decision to put it down at 45% and never pick it back up again. <br><br>Not for me. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6159265917102416099" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2022596518" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2022596518" />
    <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments"><img alt="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554228831p2/67920559.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2022596518?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments">Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=lgbtq">lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=thin-line-between-love-and-hate">thin-line-between-love-and-hate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=sexual-tension">sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=its-getting-hot-in-here">its-getting-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2022596518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9998710221323945964"><b> <i>"We're like lightning and thunder, inherently different but alike enough to share the same sky</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495379720ra/22811975.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495379721ra/22811976.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495379721ra/22811977.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>If there is one thing that Krista and Becca Ritchie were unconditionally made for - It's to write stories that will complete and fill your heart.<br/>This book made me fall in love even more with the Hales, Cobalts and Meadows and after finishing the Addicted Series, I didn't even know that was possible. <br/>______________<br/><br/><b>
  <u>The Romance</u>
</b><br/>First things first, Maximoff Hale and Farrow Keene are a ship that I am </span>
  <span id="freeText9998710221323945964" style="display:none"><b> <i>"We're like lightning and thunder, inherently different but alike enough to share the same sky</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495379720ra/22811975.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495379721ra/22811976.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495379721ra/22811977.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>If there is one thing that Krista and Becca Ritchie were unconditionally made for - It's to write stories that will complete and fill your heart.<br>This book made me fall in love even more with the Hales, Cobalts and Meadows and after finishing the Addicted Series, I didn't even know that was possible. <br>______________<br><br><b>
  <u>The Romance</u>
</b><br>First things first, Maximoff Hale and Farrow Keene are a ship that I am whole-heartedly willing to go down with. So jot that down. <br> The banter that these two have made me laugh and swoon in the span of 0.5 seconds. <br>I genuinely loved them, however I felt in the start - I couldn't get behind their chemistry as much as I did with the other characters in the past. It felt a bit rushed for me - but I overcame that pretty fast after chapter 18... because of all the flying fuckity fucks out there, boy did that chapter make me feel the heat. <br><br><br><b>
  <u>The Family</u>
</b><br>This one was the big one for me. &lt;3<br>The bonds within these three families are so strong that you can't help but feel it when you read. It is written in such an epic soul devouring way that I found myself smiling at the slightest things.<br><br><i>Public Service Announcement:</i> Xander and Luna Hale are to be protected with your life. They are angels and cinnamon rolls. No harm can come to them. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496348765ra/22903714.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496348765ra/22903715.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496348765ra/22903716.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I cannot wait to see more of these families in the upcoming books in the series. I know Krista and Becca wrote on their tumblr that their dream would be to write a story for each and every one of these characters - but it all depends on the feedback that these three novels get. <br><br>I smiled at all the moments where we saw the other characters and understood them more. It hurt and made me so happy seeing Moffy all grown up and doing exactly what Lo had talked about at the end of Some Kind Of Perfect. They all grew up and I am so proud of the Fizzle Force because we got to see it all happen. <br><br><b>
  <u>The Plot</u>
</b><br>There were lots of different elements that lined up and made this quite an interesting read. The sexual tension between Moffy and Farrow was kept through and through and I loved that element. But we also got a few snapshots of the other side characters lives. I NEED TO KNOW CHARLIE FUCKING COBALTS STORY!! <br><br>One thing that slowly had to grow on me was the stylistic device of breaking the fourth wall. Especially in Moffy's POV - he tended to talk to the audience and I ended up surprising myself and understanding why it was written that way during the end. <br><br>The twist that came right during the end felt a bit off to me. The way it was handled made room for it being a story arc in the next novel and I'm interested to see how it will be dealt with. Especially with the OG six.<br><br>Overall, Damaged Like Us gave me such a smile and I really did miss these characters and their parents more than I anticipated. All of them have made a home in my heart and I dont know if I will ever be able to get rid of them... I would never want to. <br><br>Bonus Edit:<br><br>(One of the main plot-lines was between Moffy and his father and prior to the release, I made an edit of both of them and after finishing reading DLU, this edit means so so so much more than when I made it.)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498648851i/23147316._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498648851i/23147317._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498648851i/23147318._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9998710221323945964" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/881503600" />
    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/881503600?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=forbidden">forbidden</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2017-books">2017-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=5-star-2017">5-star-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=october-2017">october-2017</a>
          </div>
